🙏 Saint Name	Swami Guru Sharanand Ji
📍 Place	Not specified
🏷 Overlay Text	Swami Guru Sharanand Ji • India
📝 What they said (summary)	Thanks Kashinath Mishra Ji for uniting the entire saint community. Says Mishra Ji has taken the sankalp (vow) to unite the whole world. Expresses deep gratitude. काशीनाथ मिश्रा जी का आभार — सबको एकजुट करने की मोहिम छेड़ी है, पूरा विश्व एक करने का संकल्प लिया है।
Key Quote(s):

"परम आदरणीय काशीनाथ मिश्रा जी का आभार व्यक्त करता हूं जिन्होंने हमें आपको मेरे पूरे परिवार को एकजुट करने की मोहिम छेड़ी है"
Translation: "I express gratitude to the most revered Kashinath Mishra Ji who has launched a campaign to unite our entire family."

"पूरा विश्व एक करने का संकल्प आदरणीय परम आदरणीय मिश्रा जी ने लिया है — मैं इनका बहुत-बहुत आभारी हूं"
Translation: "The most revered Mishra Ji has taken the vow to unite the whole world — I am deeply grateful to him."

📝 What they said (summary)	A deeply experienced 86+ year old former RSS Pracharak and engineer. Says Pandit Ji has taken a great vow (prann). Says through Pandit Ji, the dark age of Kaliyug will end. Calls it a good effort that all should support. Praises Pandit Ji for gathering all sampradayas (sects) together. पंडित जी ने प्रण किया है, कलिकाल समाप्त होगा, अच्छा प्रयत्न है, सब सम्प्रदायों को एकत्रित किया।
Key Quote(s):

"ऐसा ही पंडित जी ने प्रण किया है"
Translation: "Just like that, Pandit Ji has taken this vow."

"पंडित जी के माध्यम से कलिकाल का घोर समय समाप्त होने पर"
Translation: "Through Pandit Ji, when the dark time of Kaliyug ends..."

"ये पंडित का अच्छा प्रयत्न है इसको सहयोग करते हुए"
Translation: "This is a good effort by Pandit Ji — we should all support it."

"ये विचार पंडित जी ने आप लोगों को सभी संप्रदायों को एकत्रित किया"
Translation: "Pandit Ji has gathered all of you from all sects together through this vision."

📝 What they said (summary)	Addresses Mishra Ji with highest honorific — "Param Sammanneey Brahma Nishth Tatva Vakta Shri Vishwanath Mishra Ji." Says Mishra Ji's prophecies (Bhavishya Malika) have been proven true in the past, are being proven in the present, and WILL be proven in the future. मिश्रा जी की भविष्यवाणी अक्षरशः पूर्व में सत्य हुई, वर्तमान में हो रही, भविष्य में भी होगी।
Key Quote(s):

"परम सम्माननीय ब्रह्म निष्ठ तत्व वक्ता श्री विश्वनाथ मिश्रा जी एवं उपस्थित सभी संतों को यथा योग्य दंडवत प्रणाम"
Translation: "Dandavat pranam to the supremely respected Brahma-Nishtha orator Shri Vishwanath Mishra Ji and all saints present."

"परम सम्माननीय मिश्रा जी द्वारा जो श्रवण नित्यम... जो भविष्यवाणी अक्षर शः पूर्व में सत्य हुई है वर्तमान में सत्य हो रही है और भविष्य में भी यह होने वाला ही है"
Translation: "The prophecies presented by the most respected Mishra Ji have been proven true letter-by-letter in the past, are being proven true in the present, and WILL come true in the future as well."

Translation: "I want to thank their (Mishra Ji's) volunteers — they handled this massive saint conference so systematically that there was no room for complaint."

Clip 3.6
Field	Detail
⏱ Start	02:17:38
⏱ End	02:27:45
🙏 Saint Name	Mahant Ram Sharan Das Ji
📍 Place	Gurara, Gujarat (Ram Ji Mandir, Kajgarh)
🏷 Overlay Text	Mahant Ram Sharan Das Ji • Gurara, Gujarat
📝 What they said (summary)	Praises Mishra Ji for doing "bahut sundar karya" (very beautiful work) in the tradition of the great saints. Addresses Mishra Ji directly. Praises his simplicity — "itni saralta, sabke prati sambhaav, hansta hua mukhda" (such simplicity, equal treatment to all, smiling face). Says "Dhanya hai Mishra Ji ko" — Blessed is Mishra Ji. Prays for his longevity — "hamari aayush — hum jo bhi jab tab karte hain thoda unko bhi Bhagwan deve." मिश्रा जी ने बहुत सुंदर कार्य किया, इतनी सरलता और समभाव, धन्य हैं मिश्रा जी, भगवान इनको लम्बी आयु दे।
Key Quote(s):

"उसी परंपरा को ध्यान में रख हुए हमारे श्री मिश्रा जी बहुत सुंदर कार्य किए"
Translation: "Keeping that tradition in mind, our Shri Mishra Ji has done very beautiful work."

"इतनी सरलता सबके प्रति समभाव... हंसता हुआ मुखड़ा"
Translation: "Such simplicity, equal treatment to all... a smiling face."

"धन्य है मिश्रा जी को हमारी आयुष — हम जो भी जब तब करते हैं थोड़ा उनको भी भगवान देवे"
Translation: "Blessed is Mishra Ji — whatever lifespan we have, may God give some to him as well (praying for his long life)."

Clip 3.7 — ⭐ MOST EXTENSIVE CLIP IN VIDEO 3
Field	Detail
⏱ Start	02:32:33
⏱ End	02:49:00
🙏 Saint Name	Vrindavan Sant (Banke Bihari Sevak)
📍 Place	Vrindavan, Uttar Pradesh
🏷 Overlay Text	Vrindavan Sant (Banke Bihari Sevak) • Vrindavan
📝 What they said (summary)	His ENTIRE speech (~17 minutes) is practically a tribute to Kashinath Mishra Ji. Honors him as "Sarad." Says in 3 hours Mishra Ji never once forgot Govind — every word, every action reminded of Madhav. Calls him "LOH PURUSH" (Iron Man) — his face shows no wrinkle of worry, only ease, harmony and unity. Says it's Mishra Ji's supreme fortune that so many saints are with him. Notes he never saw Mishra Ji use aggressive/harsh speech. Offers financial contribution for the seva. Prays for his willpower to remain steady forever. मिश्रा जी को "सरद" के रूप में सम्मान, 3 घंटे में गोविंद की विस्मृति नहीं, "लोह पुरुष" कहा, चेहरे पर शिकन नहीं, सहजता-समरसता-एकता, हृदय से प्रणाम।
Key Quote(s):

"मैं अपने मिश्रा जी को सरद के रूप में सम्मान करता हूं"
Translation: "I honor my Mishra Ji as 'Sarad' (a title of deep respect)."

"मिश्रा जी ने अभी तीन घंटे में कभी भी गोविंद की विस्मृति व्यक्त नहीं कर पाए... प्रत्येक क्रिया में वाणी के प्रत्येक आलाप में माधव की स्मृति दिलाते हैं"
Translation: "In 3 hours Mishra Ji never once forgot Govind — in every action, every note of his speech, he reminds of Madhav."

"वह एक लोह पुरुष के रूप से बात कर रहा है... इनके चेहरे पर थोड़ी भी शिकन नहीं है... सहजता समरसता एकता"
Translation: "He speaks like an Iron Man... there is not even a single wrinkle of worry on his face... simplicity, harmony, unity."

"मिश्रा जी का परम सौभाग्य है कि इतने संत सब आपके साथ हैं"
Translation: "It is Mishra Ji's supreme fortune that so many saints are all with him."

"कोई ओजस वाणी का प्रयोग करते नहीं देखा"
Translation: "I have never seen him use aggressive/harsh speech."

"मिश्रा जी को हृदय से धन्यवाद... मिश्रा जी को सेवा के लिए थोड़ी सी [धनराशि]"
Translation: "Heartfelt thanks to Mishra Ji... [offering] a small financial contribution for Mishra Ji's seva."

"इनका विल पावर सदैव एक रस बना रहे... इनको कभी नींद ना आ जाए... मैं इनको हृदय से प्रणाम करता हूं"
Translation: "May his willpower remain steadfast forever... may he never fall asleep (in his mission)... I bow to him from my heart."

Clip 3.9 — ⭐ POETIC NAME INTERPRETATION
Field	Detail
⏱ Start	03:08:48
⏱ End	03:20:21
🙏 Saint Name	Neelkanth Shivcharya Dhareshwar Maharaj Ji (Adi Math Sansthan)
📍 Place	Maharashtra
🏷 Overlay Text	Neelkanth Shivcharya Dhareshwar Maharaj • Maharashtra
📝 What they said (summary)	Gives a brilliant poetic interpretation of Mishra Ji's name: "MISHRA means the one who MIXES" — he unites Shankaracharya followers, Madhvacharya followers, Shivcharyas, Warkaris, all saints, all Mata Ji's — "sabko milakar ek achchi si khichdi banayi!" (mixed them all into a beautiful khichdi!). Says even Shiv Paramatma himself has come to taste this khichdi! Also interprets KASHINATH: "Kashi ka matlab hai SHIKA — Learn!" — Kashinath means the Lord of Learning. "मिश्रा" मतलब मिश्र = इकट्ठा करने वाला — शंकराचार्य, मधवाचार्य, शिवाचार्य, वारकरी, सब संतों को मिलाकर अच्छी खिचड़ी बनाई! "काशीनाथ" = काशी = शिका = सीखो!
Key Quote(s):

"ये शर्मा जी को भेज दिया भगवान ने अब मिश्रा जी को — और ये मिश्रा काम कर रहे हैं — मिश्रा ऐसा मिश्र मतलब इकट्ठा — वो शंकराचार्य को मिलाते है मधवा जी को मिलाते हैं हमारे जैसे शिवाचार्य को मिलाते है ये वारकरी लोग है उनको भी मिलाते हैं — अब सब संतों को मिलाते है माता जी को मिला — सबको मिलाकर इन्होंने एक अच्छी सी खिचड़ी बनाई है!"
Translation: "God sent Sharma Ji, now Mishra Ji — and this MISHRA is doing the work — MISHRA means MIXER/COMBINER — he combines Shankaracharya's followers, Madhva's followers, Shivcharyas like us, the Warkari people — he combines ALL saints, all Mata Ji's — he has mixed them all into a beautiful KHICHDI!"

"और इस खिचड़ी का आस्वाद लेने के लिए स्वयं शिव परमात्मा तो आए ही है"
Translation: "And to taste this khichdi, even Lord Shiv Paramatma himself has come!"

"जब वोह बोले उसी वक्त हमने बोल दिया — अरे यह तो काशीनाथ है — काशी का मतलब है शिका"
Translation: "The moment he spoke, I immediately said — this is KASHINATH! — KASHI means LEARN (shiksha)!"

Clip 3.10
Field	Detail
⏱ Start	03:28:46
⏱ End	03:36:16
🙏 Saint Name	Sant Dada Ji (Gau Rakshak — Cow Protector)
📍 Place	Satara District, Maharashtra
🏷 Overlay Text	Sant Dada Ji (Gau Rakshak) • Satara, Maharashtra
📝 What they said (summary)	A fiery gau rakshak (cow protector) with 57+ criminal cases filed against him for cow protection work. Says from his TRUE HEART — "Mishra Ji ka kaam, this should have been done LONG AGO by sadhus and saints, but no one did it. He is doing it now. His UPKAAR (obligation/grace) upon us is IMMENSE." सच्चे दिल से कहता हूं — यह काम बहुत पहले साधु संतों को करना चाहिए था, नहीं किया तो अब मिश्रा जी कर रहे हैं — इसका हमारे ऊपर बहुत उपकार है।
Key Quote(s):

"मैं मिश्रा जी का कर सच्चे तो दिल से — मेरे को बहुत आनंद हुआ — ऐसा काम बहुत पूर्व पहले अपने लोगों ने करना चाहिए था साधु संतो ने करना चाहिए था मगर नहीं किया"
Translation: "From my true heart about Mishra Ji — I am overjoyed — this work should have been done much earlier by our people, by sadhus and saints, but no one did it."

"तो यह काम अभी कर रहे — इसका हमारे ऊपर इतना उपकार है — बहुत उपकार है"
Translation: "So he is doing this work now — his grace/obligation upon us is THIS MUCH — it is IMMENSE."

Clip 3.11 — ⭐ "GOD'S CHOSEN INSTRUMENT"
Field	Detail
⏱ Start	03:41:29
⏱ End	03:52:48
🙏 Saint Name	Doctor Babu Sant Maharaj
📍 Place	Ujjain, Madhya Pradesh
🏷 Overlay Text	Doctor Babu Sant Maharaj • Ujjain
📝 What they said (summary)	The most spiritually profound clip in Video 3. Looks at Kashinath Ji sitting for 5+ hours on one seat and asks "whose power is this?" Declares: "Bhagwan ne Mishra Ji ko NIMITT banaya hai — kisiko achcha nimitt har kisi ko nahi banate — jo KHAAS hota hai na WAHI nimitt banaya jaata hai!" (God made Mishra Ji His INSTRUMENT — not everyone is made an instrument — only the SPECIAL one is chosen!). Then tells the story of Mahadev becoming a Gopi to see Krishna's Raas — says just like Mahadev couldn't resist coming uninvited, "hum sab bhi apne aap aaye hain" — we all came on our own, drawn by divine pull. Says "hum sab ka ananth janmon se Mishra Ji se prarabdh tha" — our connection with Mishra Ji spans infinite past lives. Finally: "Mishra Ji ko bahut bahut dhanyavaad." भगवान ने मिश्र जी को निमित्त बनाया — जो खास होता है वही निमित्त बनाया जाता है। अनंत जन्मों से मिश्रा जी से प्रारब्ध था। बहुत-बहुत धन्यवाद।
Key Quote(s):

"साढ़े चार-पांच घंटे बैठे हुए हैं — य किसकी देन है — किसकी शक्ति है"
Translation: "He has been sitting for 4.5-5 hours — whose gift is this — whose power is this?"

"निमित्त बनाया है भगवान ने — मिश्र जी को निमित्त बनाया है — किसी को अच्छा निमित्त हर किसी को नहीं बनाते — जो खास होता है ना वही निमित्त बनाया जाता है"
Translation: "God has made Mishra Ji His INSTRUMENT — not everyone is made a good instrument — only the one who is SPECIAL is chosen as the instrument!"

"हम सबका अनंत जन्मों से मिश्रा जी से प्रारब्ध था — इसके सिवा बिना प्रारब्ध के कुछ नहीं होता है"
Translation: "All of us have had a karmic connection (prarabdh) with Mishra Ji since infinite past lives — without such karmic destiny, nothing happens."

"कैसे कहूं — मिश्रा जी को बहुत-बहुत धन्यवाद"
Translation: "How do I even express it — immense, immense thanks to Mishra Ji."
